<pr_description>
TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimesBetween does not handle DST properly
Hi,
I think I found a problem with the generation of the fire times when crossing the DST date.
I can reproduce it on the 3.2.4 with .NET 4.7.2.

```
 DateTime startDateTime = new DateTime(2020, 10, 25);
            DateTimeOffset startDateTimeOffset = new DateTimeOffset(startDateTime);
            int daysAhead = 3;

            TriggerBuilder triggerBuilder = TriggerBuilder.Create()
                .WithIdentity("id")
                .ForJob("job")
                .StartAt(new DateTimeOffset(startDateTime.AddMinutes(1).AddSeconds(5)))
                .WithDailyTimeIntervalSchedule(
                    scheduleBuilder =>
                    {
                        scheduleBuilder.OnEveryDay().WithIntervalInHours(24);
                        scheduleBuilder
                            .StartingDailyAt(new TimeOfDay(0, 1, 5))
                            .EndingDailyAt(new TimeOfDay(23, 59, 59))
                            .WithMisfireHandlingInstructionDoNothing();
                    });

            IReadOnlyList<DateTimeOffset> fireTimes =
                TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimesBetween((
                IOperableTrigger)triggerBuilder.Build(),
                null,
                startDateTimeOffset,
                startDateTimeOffset.AddDays(daysAhead));

            Assert.AreEqual(new DateTimeOffset(new DateTime(2020, 10, 25, 0, 1, 5)), fireTimes.First().LocalDateTime);
            Assert.AreEqual(new DateTimeOffset(new DateTime(2020, 10, 26, 0, 1, 5)), fireTimes.Skip(1).First().LocalDateTime);
            Assert.AreEqual(new DateTimeOffset(new DateTime(2020, 10, 27, 0, 1, 5)), fireTimes.Skip(2).First().LocalDateTime);
```

Expected: According to the setup I would expect 3 dates given in the assert.

Actual: 4 dates, with additional DateTime(2020, 10, 25, 23, 1, 5).


kind regards,
Kamil

</pr_description>

    22	using Quartz.Spi;
    23	
    24	namespace Quartz;
    25	
    26	/// <summary>
    27	/// Convenience and utility methods for simplifying the construction and
    28	/// configuration of <see cref="ITrigger" />s and DateTimeOffsetOffsets.
    29	/// </summary>
    30	/// <seealso cref="ICronTrigger" />
    31	/// <seealso cref="ISimpleTrigger" />
    32	/// <author>James House</author>
    33	/// <author>Marko Lahma (.NET)</author>
    34	public static class TriggerUtils
    35	{
    36	    /// <summary>
    37	    /// Returns a list of Dates that are the next fire times of a
    38	    /// <see cref="ITrigger" />.
    39	    /// The input trigger will be cloned before any work is done, so you need
    40	    /// not worry about its state being altered by this method.
    41	    /// </summary>
    42	    /// <param name="trigger">The trigger upon which to do the work</param>
    43	    /// <param name="calendar">The calendar to apply to the trigger's schedule</param>
    44	    /// <param name="numTimes">The number of next fire times to produce</param>
    45	    public static IReadOnlyList<DateTimeOffset> ComputeFireTimes(IOperableTrigger trigger, ICalendar? calendar, int numTimes)
    46	    {
    47	        List<DateTimeOffset> lst = new List<DateTimeOffset>();
    48	
    49	        IOperableTrigger t = (IOperableTrigger) trigger.Clone();
    50	
    51	        if (t.GetNextFireTimeUtc() is null || !t.GetNextFireTimeUtc().HasValue)
    52	        {
    53	            t.ComputeFirstFireTimeUtc(calendar);
    54	        }
    55	
    56	        for (int i = 0; i < numTimes; i++)
    57	        {
    58	            DateTimeOffset? d = t.GetNextFireTimeUtc();
    59	            if (d.HasValue)
    60	            {
    61	                lst.Add(d.Value);
    62	                t.Triggered(calendar);
    63	            }
    64	            else
    65	            {
    66	                break;
    67	            }
    68	        }
    69	
    70	        return lst.AsReadOnly();
    71	    }
    72	
    73	    /// <summary>
    74	    /// Compute the <see cref="DateTimeOffset" /> that is 1 second after the Nth firing of
    75	    /// the given <see cref="ITrigger" />, taking the trigger's associated
    76	    /// <see cref="ICalendar" /> into consideration.
    77	    /// </summary>
    78	    /// <remarks>
    79	    /// The input trigger will be cloned before any work is done, so you need
    80	    /// not worry about its state being altered by this method.
    81	    /// </remarks>
    82	    /// <param name="trigger">The trigger upon which to do the work</param>
    83	    /// <param name="calendar">The calendar to apply to the trigger's schedule</param>
    84	    /// <param name="numberOfTimes">The number of next fire times to produce</param>
    85	    /// <returns>the computed Date, or null if the trigger (as configured) will not fire that many times</returns>
    86	    public static DateTimeOffset? ComputeEndTimeToAllowParticularNumberOfFirings(IOperableTrigger trigger, ICalendar? calendar, int numberOfTimes)
    87	    {
    88	        IOperableTrigger t = (IOperableTrigger) trigger.Clone();
    89	
    90	        if (t.GetNextFireTimeUtc() is null)
    91	        {
    92	            t.ComputeFirstFireTimeUtc(calendar);
    93	        }
    94	
    95	        int c = 0;
    96	        DateTimeOffset? endTime = null;
    97	
    98	        for (int i = 0; i < numberOfTimes; i++)
    99	        {
   100	            DateTimeOffset? d = t.GetNextFireTimeUtc();
   101	            if (d is not null)
   102	            {
   103	                c++;
   104	                t.Triggered(calendar);
   105	                if (c == numberOfTimes)
   106	                {
   107	                    endTime = d;
   108	                }
   109	            }
   110	            else
   111	            {
   112	                break;
   113	            }
   114	        }
   115	
   116	        if (endTime is null)
   117	        {
   118	            return null;
   119	        }
   120	
   121	        endTime = endTime.Value.AddSeconds(1);
   122	
   123	        return endTime;
   124	    }
   125	
   126	
   127	    /// <summary>
   128	    /// Returns a list of Dates that are the next fire times of a  <see cref="ITrigger" />
   129	    /// that fall within the given date range. The input trigger will be cloned
   130	    /// before any work is done, so you need not worry about its state being
   131	    /// altered by this method.
   132	    /// <para>
   133	    /// NOTE: if this is a trigger that has previously fired within the given
   134	    /// date range, then firings which have already occurred will not be listed
   135	    /// in the output List.
   136	    /// </para>
   137	    /// </summary>
   138	    /// <param name="trigger">The trigger upon which to do the work</param>
   139	    /// <param name="calendar">The calendar to apply to the trigger's schedule</param>
   140	    /// <param name="from">The starting date at which to find fire times</param>
   141	    /// <param name="to">The ending date at which to stop finding fire times</param>
   142	    public static IReadOnlyList<DateTimeOffset> ComputeFireTimesBetween(IOperableTrigger trigger, ICalendar? calendar, DateTimeOffset from, DateTimeOffset to)
   143	    {
   144	        List<DateTimeOffset> lst = new List<DateTimeOffset>();
   145	
   146	        IOperableTrigger t = (IOperableTrigger) trigger.Clone();
   147	
   148	        if (t.GetNextFireTimeUtc() is null || !t.GetNextFireTimeUtc().HasValue)
   149	        {
   150	            // Only preserve the trigger's own StartTimeUtc if it falls within
   151	            // the query range [from, to]. This ensures fire times stay aligned
   152	            // with the trigger's configured schedule, while still supporting
   153	            // arbitrary date range queries where from/to define the window.
   154	            if (t.StartTimeUtc < from || t.StartTimeUtc > to)
   155	            {
   156	                t.StartTimeUtc = from;
   157	            }
   158	            if (!t.EndTimeUtc.HasValue || t.EndTimeUtc.Value > to)
   159	            {
   160	                t.EndTimeUtc = to;
   161	            }
   162	            t.ComputeFirstFireTimeUtc(calendar);
   163	        }
   164	
   165	        // TODO: this method could be more efficient by using logic specific
   166	        //        to the type of trigger ...
   167	        while (true)
   168	        {
   169	            DateTimeOffset? d = t.GetNextFireTimeUtc();
   170	            if (d.HasValue)
   171	            {
   172	                if (d.Value < from)
   173	                {
   174	                    t.Triggered(calendar);
   175	                    continue;
   176	                }
   177	                if (d.Value > to)
   178	                {
   179	                    break;
   180	                }
   181	                lst.Add(d.Value);
   182	                t.Triggered(calendar);
   183	            }
   184	            else
   185	            {
   186	                break;
   187	            }
   188	        }
   189	        return lst.AsReadOnly();
   190	    }
   191	}

    22	using Quartz.Util;
    23	
    24	namespace Quartz.Impl.Triggers;
    25	
    26	/// <summary>
    27	/// A concrete implementation of DailyTimeIntervalTrigger that is used to fire a <see cref="IJobDetail"/>
    28	/// based upon daily repeating time intervals.
    29	/// </summary>
    30	/// <remarks>
    31	/// <para>
    32	/// The trigger will fire every N (<see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger.RepeatInterval"/> ) seconds, minutes or hours
    33	/// (see <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger.RepeatInterval"/>) during a given time window on specified days of the week.
    34	/// </para>
    35	/// <para>
    36	/// For example#1, a trigger can be set to fire every 72 minutes between 8:00 and 11:00 everyday. It's fire times would
    37	/// be 8:00, 9:12, 10:24, then next day would repeat: 8:00, 9:12, 10:24 again.
    38	/// </para>
    39	/// <para>
    40	/// For example#2, a trigger can be set to fire every 23 minutes between 9:20 and 16:47 Monday through Friday.
    41	/// </para>
    42	/// <para>
    43	/// On each day, the starting fire time is reset to startTimeOfDay value, and then it will add repeatInterval value to it until
    44	/// the endTimeOfDay is reached. If you set daysOfWeek values, then fire time will only occur during those week days period. Again,
    45	/// remember this trigger will reset fire time each day with startTimeOfDay, regardless of your interval or endTimeOfDay!
    46	/// </para>
    47	/// <para>
    48	/// The default values for fields if not set are: startTimeOfDay defaults to 00:00:00, the endTimeOfDay default to 23:59:59,
    49	/// and daysOfWeek is default to every day. The startTime default to current time-stamp now, while endTime has not value.
    50	/// </para>
    51	/// <para>
    52	/// If startTime is before startTimeOfDay, then startTimeOfDay will be used and startTime has no affect other than to specify
    53	/// the first day of firing. Else if startTime is  after startTimeOfDay, then the first fire time for that day will be the next
    54	/// interval after the startTime. For example, if you set startingTimeOfDay=9am, endingTimeOfDay=11am, interval=15 mins, and startTime=9:33am,
    55	/// then the next fire time will be 9:45pm. Note also that if you do not set startTime value, the trigger builder will default to current time, and current time
    56	/// maybe before or after the startTimeOfDay! So be aware how you set your startTime.
    57	/// </para>
    58	/// <para>
    59	/// This trigger also supports a "repeatCount" feature to limit the number of times the trigger
    60	/// fires per day. Setting repeatCount=0 means the trigger will fire once per day at startTimeOfDay.
    61	/// Setting repeatCount=N means the trigger will fire N+1 times per day (the initial fire plus N
    62	/// repeats), then advance to the next valid day and repeat. Unlike SimpleTrigger which uses
    63	/// repeatCount as a global total, DailyTimeIntervalTrigger applies repeatCount per day. The
    64	/// default value of repeatCount is set to REPEAT_INDEFINITELY.
    65	/// </para>
    66	/// </remarks>
    67	/// <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger"/>
    68	/// <see cref="DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder"/>
    69	/// <since>2.0</since>
    70	/// <author>James House</author>
    71	/// <author>Zemian Deng saltnlight5@gmail.com</author>
    72	/// <author>Nuno Maia (.NET)</author>
    73	[Serializable]
    74	#pragma warning disable CA1708
    75	public sealed class DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl : AbstractTrigger, IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger
    76	#pragma warning restore CA1708
    77	{
    78	    /// <summary>
    79	    /// Used to indicate the 'repeat count' of the trigger is indefinite. Or in
    80	    /// other words, the trigger should repeat continually until the trigger's
    81	    /// ending timestamp.
    82	    /// </summary>
    83	    public const int RepeatIndefinitely = -1;
    84	    private DateTimeOffset startTimeUtc;
    85	    private DateTimeOffset? endTimeUtc;
    86	    private DateTimeOffset? nextFireTimeUtc;
    87	    private DateTimeOffset? previousFireTimeUtc;
    88	    private int repeatInterval = 1;
    89	    private IntervalUnit repeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Minute;
    90	    private HashSet<DayOfWeek> daysOfWeek = null!;
    91	    private TimeOfDay startTimeOfDay = null!;
    92	    private TimeOfDay endTimeOfDay = null!;
    93	    private bool complete;
    94	    private int repeatCount = RepeatIndefinitely;
    95	    internal TimeZoneInfo? timeZone;
    96	
    97	    // Serializing TimeZones is tricky in .NET Core. This helper will ensure that we get the same timezone on a given platform,
    98	    // but there's not yet a good method of serializing/deserializing timezones cross-platform since Windows timezone IDs don't
    99	    // match IANA tz IDs (https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_tz_database_time_zones). This feature is coming, but depending
   100	    // on timelines, it may be worth doign the mapping here.
   101	    // More info: https://github.com/dotnet/corefx/issues/7757
   102	    private string? timeZoneInfoId
   103	    {
   104	        get => timeZone?.Id;
   105	        set => timeZone = value is null ? null : TimeZoneInfo.FindSystemTimeZoneById(value);
   106	    }

   222	    /// <summary>
   223	    /// Create a <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger" /> that will occur at the given time,
   224	    /// fire the identified job and repeat at the given
   225	    /// interval until the given end time.
   226	    /// </summary>
   227	    /// <param name="name"></param>
   228	    /// <param name="group"></param>
   229	    /// <param name="jobName"></param>
   230	    /// <param name="jobGroup"></param>

   232	    /// <param name="endTimeUtc">A <see cref="DateTimeOffset" /> set to the time for the <see cref="ITrigger" />to quit repeat firing.</param>
   233	    /// <param name="startTimeOfDayUtc">The <see cref="TimeOfDay" /> that the repeating should begin occurring.</param>
   234	    /// <param name="endTimeOfDayUtc">The <see cref="TimeOfDay" /> that the repeating should stop occurring.</param>
   235	    /// <param name="intervalUnit">The repeat interval unit. The only intervals that are valid for this type of trigger are <see cref="IntervalUnit.Second"/>, <see cref="IntervalUnit.Minute"/>, and <see cref="IntervalUnit.Hour"/>.</param>
   236	    /// <param name="repeatInterval">The number of milliseconds to pause between the repeat firing.</param>
   237	    /// <param name="timeProvider">Time provider instance to use, defaults to <see cref="TimeProvider.System"/></param>
   238	    /// <exception cref="ArgumentNullException"><paramref name="name"/>, <paramref name="group"/>, <paramref name="jobName"/> or <paramref name="jobGroup"/> are <see langword="null"/>.</exception>
   239	    public DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl(
   240	        string name,
   241	        string group,
   242	        string jobName,
   243	        string jobGroup,
   244	        DateTimeOffset startTimeUtc,
   245	        DateTimeOffset? endTimeUtc,
   246	        TimeOfDay startTimeOfDayUtc,
   247	        TimeOfDay endTimeOfDayUtc,
   248	        IntervalUnit intervalUnit,
   249	        int repeatInterval,
   250	        TimeProvider? timeProvider = null)
   251	        : base(name, group, jobName, jobGroup, timeProvider ?? TimeProvider.System)
   252	    {

   254	        EndTimeUtc = endTimeUtc;

   258	        EndTimeOfDay = endTimeOfDayUtc;

   260	
   261	    /// <summary>
   262	    /// The time at which the <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger" /> should occur.
   263	    /// </summary>
   264	    public override DateTimeOffset StartTimeUtc
   265	    {
   266	        get
   267	        {
   268	            if (startTimeUtc == DateTimeOffset.MinValue)
   269	            {
   270	                startTimeUtc = TimeProvider.GetUtcNow();
   271	            }
   272	            return startTimeUtc;
   273	        }
   274	        set
   275	        {
   276	            if (value == DateTimeOffset.MinValue)
   277	            {
   278	                Throw.ArgumentException("Start time cannot be DateTimeOffset.MinValue");
   279	            }
   280	
   281	            DateTimeOffset? eTime = EndTimeUtc;
   282	            if (eTime is not null && eTime < value)
   283	            {
   284	                Throw.ArgumentException("End time cannot be before start time");
   285	            }
   286	
   287	            startTimeUtc = value;
   288	        }
   289	    }
   290	
   291	    /// <summary>
   292	    /// the time at which the <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger" /> should quit repeating.
   293	    /// </summary>
   294	    /// <see cref="DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl.FinalFireTimeUtc"/>
   295	    public override DateTimeOffset? EndTimeUtc
   296	    {
   297	        get => endTimeUtc;
   298	        set
   299	        {
   300	            DateTimeOffset sTime = StartTimeUtc;
   301	            if (value is not null && sTime > value)
   302	            {
   303	                Throw.ArgumentException("End time cannot be before start time");
   304	            }
   305	
   306	            endTimeUtc = value;
   307	        }
   308	    }
   309	
   310	    /// <summary>
   311	    /// Get the number of times per day this trigger should repeat.
   312	    /// Setting to 0 means fire once per day; setting to N means fire N+1 times per day.
   313	    /// </summary>
   314	    public int RepeatCount
   315	    {
   316	        get => repeatCount;
   317	        set
   318	        {
   319	            if (value < 0 && value != RepeatIndefinitely)
   320	            {
   321	                Throw.ArgumentException("Repeat count must be >= 0, use the constant RepeatIndefinitely for infinite.");
   322	            }
   323	
   324	            repeatCount = value;
   325	        }
   326	    }
   327	
   328	    /// <summary>
   329	    /// the interval unit - the time unit on with the interval applies.
   330	    /// </summary>
   331	    /// <remarks>
   332	    /// The repeat interval unit. The only intervals that are valid for this type of trigger are
   333	    /// <see cref="IntervalUnit.Second"/>, <see cref="IntervalUnit.Minute"/>, and <see cref="IntervalUnit.Hour"/>.
   334	    /// </remarks>
   335	    public IntervalUnit RepeatIntervalUnit
   336	    {
   337	        get => repeatIntervalUnit;
   338	        set
   339	        {
   340	            if (!(value == IntervalUnit.Second ||
   341	                  value == IntervalUnit.Minute ||
   342	                  value == IntervalUnit.Hour))
   343	            {
   344	                Throw.ArgumentException("Invalid repeat IntervalUnit (must be Second, Minute or Hour)");
   345	            }
   346	
   347	            repeatIntervalUnit = value;
   348	        }
   349	    }
   350	
   351	    /// <summary>
   352	    /// the time interval that will be added to the <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger" />'s
   353	    /// fire time (in the set repeat interval unit) in order to calculate the time of the
   354	    /// next trigger repeat.
   355	    /// </summary>
   356	    public int RepeatInterval
   357	    {
   358	        get => repeatInterval;
   359	        set
   360	        {
   361	            if (value < 1)
   362	            {
   363	                Throw.ArgumentException("Repeat interval must be >= 1");
   364	            }
   365	
   366	            repeatInterval = value;
   367	        }
   368	    }

   370	    /// <summary>
   371	    /// the number of times the <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger" /> has already
   372	    /// fired.
   373	    /// </summary>
   374	    public int TimesTriggered { get; set; }
   375	
   376	    public TimeZoneInfo TimeZone
   377	    {
   378	        get
   379	        {
   380	            if (timeZone is null)
   381	            {
   382	                timeZone = TimeZoneInfo.Local;
   383	            }
   384	            return timeZone;
   385	        }
   386	
   387	        set => timeZone = value;
   388	    }
   389	
   390	    protected override bool ValidateMisfireInstruction(int misfireInstruction)
   391	    {
   392	        if (misfireInstruction < Quartz.MisfireInstruction.IgnoreMisfirePolicy)
   393	        {
   394	            return false;
   395	        }
   396	        if (misfireInstruction > Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.DoNothing)
   397	        {
   398	            return false;
   399	        }
   400	
   401	        return true;
   402	    }
   403	
   404	    /// <summary>
   405	    /// Updates the <see cref="ICalendarIntervalTrigger" />'s state based on the
   406	    /// MisfireInstruction.XXX that was selected when the <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger" />
   407	    /// was created.
   408	    /// </summary>
   409	    /// <remarks>
   410	    /// If the misfire instruction is set to <see cref="MisfireInstruction.SmartPolicy" />,
   411	    /// then the following scheme will be used:
   412	    /// <ul>
   413	    ///     <li>The instruction will be interpreted as <see cref="MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.FireOnceNow" /></li>
   414	    /// </ul>
   415	    /// </remarks>
   416	    public override void UpdateAfterMisfire(ICalendar? cal)
   417	    {
   418	        int instr = MisfireInstruction;
   419	
   420	        if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.IgnoreMisfirePolicy)
   421	        {
   422	            return;
   423	        }
   424	
   425	        if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.SmartPolicy)
   426	        {
   427	            instr = Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.FireOnceNow;
   428	        }
   429	
   430	        if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.DoNothing)
   431	        {
   432	            DateTimeOffset? newFireTime = GetFireTimeAfter(TimeProvider.GetUtcNow());
   433	            while (newFireTime is not null && cal is not null && !cal.IsTimeIncluded(newFireTime.Value))
   434	            {
   435	                newFireTime = GetFireTimeAfter(newFireTime);
   436	            }
   437	            SetNextFireTimeUtc(newFireTime);
   438	        }
   439	        else if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.FireOnceNow)
   440	        {
   441	            // fire once now...
   442	            SetNextFireTimeUtc(TimeProvider.GetUtcNow());
   443	            // the new fire time afterward will magically preserve the original
   444	            // time of day for firing for day/week/month interval triggers,
   445	            // because of the way getFireTimeAfter() works - in its always restarting
   446	            // computation from the start time.
   447	        }
   448	    }
   449	
   450	    internal override void UpdateAfterMisfire(ICalendar? cal, TimeSpan misfireThreshold)
   451	    {
   452	        int instr = MisfireInstruction;
   453	
   454	        if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.IgnoreMisfirePolicy)
   455	        {
   456	            return;
   457	        }
   458	
   459	        if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.SmartPolicy)
   460	        {
   461	            instr = Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.FireOnceNow;
   462	        }
   463	
   464	        if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.DoNothing)
   465	        {
   466	            DateTimeOffset? newFireTime = GetFireTimeAfter(TimeProvider.GetUtcNow() - misfireThreshold);
   467	            while (newFireTime != null && cal != null && !cal.IsTimeIncluded(newFireTime.Value))
   468	            {
   469	                newFireTime = GetFireTimeAfter(newFireTime);
   470	            }
   471	            SetNextFireTimeUtc(newFireTime);
   472	        }
   473	        else if (instr == Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.FireOnceNow)
   474	        {
   475	            SetNextFireTimeUtc(TimeProvider.GetUtcNow());
   476	        }
   477	    }
   478	
   479	    /// <summary>
   480	    /// Called when the scheduler has decided to 'fire'
   481	    /// the trigger (execute the associated job), in order to
   482	    /// give the trigger a chance to update itself for its next
   483	    /// triggering (if any).
   484	    /// </summary>
   485	    /// <param name="calendar"></param>
   486	    /// <see cref="AbstractTrigger.ExecutionComplete"/>
   487	    public override void Triggered(ICalendar? calendar)
   488	    {
   489	        TimesTriggered++;
   490	        previousFireTimeUtc = nextFireTimeUtc;
   491	        nextFireTimeUtc = GetFireTimeAfter(nextFireTimeUtc);
   492	
   493	        while (nextFireTimeUtc is not null && calendar is not null
   494	                                       && !calendar.IsTimeIncluded(nextFireTimeUtc.Value))
   495	        {
   496	            nextFireTimeUtc = GetFireTimeAfter(nextFireTimeUtc);
   497	
   498	            if (nextFireTimeUtc is null)
   499	            {
   500	                break;
   501	            }
   502	
   503	            //avoid infinite loop
   504	            if (nextFireTimeUtc.Value.Year > TriggerConstants.YearToGiveUpSchedulingAt)
   505	            {
   506	                nextFireTimeUtc = null;
   507	            }
   508	        }
   509	
   510	        if (nextFireTimeUtc is null)
   511	        {
   512	            complete = true;
   513	        }
   514	    }
   515	
   516	    /// <summary>
   517	    ///
   518	    /// </summary>
   519	    /// <param name="calendar"></param>
   520	    /// <param name="misfireThreshold"></param>
   521	    /// <see cref="AbstractTrigger.UpdateWithNewCalendar"/>
   522	    public override void UpdateWithNewCalendar(ICalendar calendar, TimeSpan misfireThreshold)
   523	    {
   524	        nextFireTimeUtc = GetFireTimeAfter(previousFireTimeUtc);
   525	
   526	        if (nextFireTimeUtc is null || calendar is null)
   527	        {
   528	            return;
   529	        }
   530	
   531	        DateTimeOffset now = TimeProvider.GetUtcNow();
   532	        while (nextFireTimeUtc is not null && !calendar.IsTimeIncluded(nextFireTimeUtc.Value))
   533	        {
   534	            nextFireTimeUtc = GetFireTimeAfter(nextFireTimeUtc);
   535	
   536	            if (nextFireTimeUtc is null)
   537	            {
   538	                break;
   539	            }
   540	
   541	            //avoid infinite loop
   542	            if (nextFireTimeUtc.Value.Year > TriggerConstants.YearToGiveUpSchedulingAt)
   543	            {
   544	                nextFireTimeUtc = null;
   545	            }
   546	
   547	            if (nextFireTimeUtc is not null && nextFireTimeUtc < now)
   548	            {
   549	                TimeSpan diff = now - nextFireTimeUtc.Value;
   550	                if (diff >= misfireThreshold)
   551	                {
   552	                    nextFireTimeUtc = GetFireTimeAfter(nextFireTimeUtc);
   553	                }
   554	            }
   555	        }
   556	    }
   557	
   558	    /// <summary>
   559	    /// This method should not be used by the Quartz client.
   560	    /// </summary>
   561	    /// <remarks>
   562	    /// <para>
   563	    /// Called by the scheduler at the time a <see cref="ITrigger" /> is first
   564	    /// added to the scheduler, in order to have the <see cref="ITrigger" />
   565	    /// compute its first fire time, based on any associated calendar.
   566	    /// </para>
   567	    ///
   568	    /// <para>
   569	    /// After this method has been called, <see cref="ITrigger.GetNextFireTimeUtc" />
   570	    /// should return a valid answer.
   571	    /// </para>
   572	    /// </remarks>
   573	    /// <returns>
   574	    /// The first time at which the <see cref="ITrigger" /> will be fired
   575	    /// by the scheduler, which is also the same value <see cref="ITrigger.GetNextFireTimeUtc" />
   576	    /// will return (until after the first firing of the <see cref="ITrigger" />).
   577	    /// </returns>
   578	    public override DateTimeOffset? ComputeFirstFireTimeUtc(ICalendar? calendar)
   579	    {
   580	        nextFireTimeUtc = GetFireTimeAfter(StartTimeUtc.AddSeconds(-1));
   581	
   582	        // Check calendar for date-time exclusion
   583	        while (nextFireTimeUtc is not null && calendar is not null
   584	                                       && !calendar.IsTimeIncluded(nextFireTimeUtc.Value))
   585	        {
   586	            nextFireTimeUtc = GetFireTimeAfter(nextFireTimeUtc);
   587	
   588	            if (nextFireTimeUtc is null)
   589	            {
   590	                break;
   591	            }
   592	
   593	            //avoid infinite loop
   594	            if (nextFireTimeUtc.Value.Year > TriggerConstants.YearToGiveUpSchedulingAt)
   595	            {
   596	                return null;
   597	            }
   598	        }
   599	
   600	        return nextFireTimeUtc;
   601	    }
   602	
   603	    private DateTimeOffset CreateCalendarTime(DateTimeOffset dateTime)
   604	    {
   605	        return TimeZoneUtil.ConvertTime(dateTime, TimeZone);
   606	    }
   607	
   608	    /// <summary>
   609	    /// Returns the next time at which the <see cref="ITrigger" /> is scheduled to fire. If
   610	    /// the trigger will not fire again, <see langword="null" /> will be returned.  Note that
   611	    /// the time returned can possibly be in the past, if the time that was computed
   612	    /// for the trigger to next fire has already arrived, but the scheduler has not yet
   613	    /// been able to fire the trigger (which would likely be due to lack of resources
   614	    /// e.g. threads).
   615	    /// </summary>
   616	    ///<remarks>
   617	    /// The value returned is not guaranteed to be valid until after the <see cref="ITrigger" />
   618	    /// has been added to the scheduler.
   619	    /// </remarks>
   620	    /// <returns></returns>
   621	    public override DateTimeOffset? GetNextFireTimeUtc()
   622	    {
   623	        return nextFireTimeUtc;
   624	    }
   625	
   626	    /// <summary>
   627	    /// Returns the previous time at which the <see cref="ICalendarIntervalTrigger" /> fired.
   628	    /// If the trigger has not yet fired, <see langword="null" /> will be returned.
   629	    /// </summary>
   630	    public override DateTimeOffset? GetPreviousFireTimeUtc()
   631	    {
   632	        return previousFireTimeUtc;
   633	    }
   634	
   635	    /// <summary>
   636	    /// Set the next time at which the <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger" /> should fire.
   637	    /// </summary>
   638	    /// <remarks>
   639	    /// This method should not be invoked by client code.
   640	    /// </remarks>
   641	    /// <param name="value"></param>
   642	    public override void SetNextFireTimeUtc(DateTimeOffset? value)
   643	    {
   644	        nextFireTimeUtc = value;
   645	    }
   646	
   647	    /// <summary>
   648	    /// Set the previous time at which the <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger" /> fired.
   649	    /// </summary>
   650	    /// <remarks>
   651	    /// This method should not be invoked by client code.
   652	    /// </remarks>
   653	    /// <param name="previousFireTimeUtc"></param>
   654	    public override void SetPreviousFireTimeUtc(DateTimeOffset? previousFireTimeUtc)
   655	    {
   656	        this.previousFireTimeUtc = previousFireTimeUtc;
   657	    }
   658	
   659	    /// <summary>
   660	    /// Returns the next time at which the <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger" /> will
   661	    /// fire, after the given time. If the trigger will not fire after the given
   662	    /// time, <see langword="null" /> will be returned.
   663	    /// </summary>
   664	    /// <param name="afterTime"></param>
   665	    /// <returns></returns>
   666	    public override DateTimeOffset? GetFireTimeAfter(DateTimeOffset? afterTime)
   667	    {
   668	        // Check if trigger has completed or not.
   669	        if (complete)
   670	        {
   671	            return null;
   672	        }
   673	
   674	        // a. Increment afterTime by a second, so that we are comparing against a time after it!
   675	        if (afterTime is null)
   676	        {
   677	            afterTime = TimeProvider.GetUtcNow().AddSeconds(1);
   678	        }
   679	        else
   680	        {
   681	            afterTime = afterTime.Value.AddSeconds(1);
   682	        }
   683	
   684	        // make sure afterTime is at least startTime
   685	        if (afterTime < startTimeUtc)
   686	        {
   687	            afterTime = startTimeUtc;
   688	        }
   689	
   690	        // now change to local time zone
   691	        afterTime = TimeZoneUtil.ConvertTime(afterTime.Value, TimeZone);
   692	
   693	        // b.Check to see if afterTime is after endTimeOfDay or not.
   694	        // If yes, then we need to advance to next day as well.
   695	        bool afterTimePastEndTimeOfDay = false;
   696	        if (endTimeOfDay is not null)
   697	        {
   698	            afterTimePastEndTimeOfDay = afterTime.Value > endTimeOfDay.GetTimeOfDayForDate(afterTime.Value);
   699	        }
   700	
   701	        // c. now we need to move to the next valid day of week if either:
   702	        // the given time is past the end time of day, or given time is not on a valid day of week
   703	        DateTimeOffset? fireTime = AdvanceToNextDayOfWeekIfNecessary(afterTime.Value, afterTimePastEndTimeOfDay);
   704	
   705	        if (fireTime is null)
   706	        {
   707	            return null;
   708	        }
   709	
   710	        // d. Calculate and save fireTimeEndDate variable for later use
   711	        DateTimeOffset fireTimeEndDate;
   712	        if (endTimeOfDay is null)
   713	        {
   714	            fireTimeEndDate = new TimeOfDay(23, 59, 59).GetTimeOfDayForDate(fireTime.Value);
   715	        }
   716	        else
   717	        {
   718	            fireTimeEndDate = endTimeOfDay.GetTimeOfDayForDate(fireTime.Value);
   719	        }
   720	
   721	        // apply the proper offset for the end date
   722	        fireTimeEndDate = new DateTimeOffset(fireTimeEndDate.DateTime, TimeZoneUtil.GetUtcOffset(fireTimeEndDate.DateTime, TimeZone));
   723	
   724	        // e. Check fireTime against startTime or startTimeOfDay to see which go first.
   725	        DateTimeOffset fireTimeStartDate = startTimeOfDay.GetTimeOfDayForDate(fireTime.Value);
   726	
   727	        // apply the proper offset for the start date
   728	        fireTimeStartDate = new DateTimeOffset(fireTimeStartDate.DateTime, TimeZoneUtil.GetUtcOffset(fireTimeStartDate.DateTime, TimeZone));
   729	
   730	        if (fireTime < fireTimeStartDate)
   731	        {
   732	            return fireTimeStartDate.ToUniversalTime();
   733	        }
   734	
   735	        // f. Continue to calculate the fireTime by incremental unit of intervals.
   736	        // recall that if fireTime was less that fireTimeStartDate, we didn't get this far
   737	        DateTimeOffset startOfDayUtc = TimeZoneUtil.ConvertTime(fireTimeStartDate, TimeZone);
   738	        long secondsAfterStart = (long) (fireTime.Value - startOfDayUtc).TotalSeconds;
   739	        long repeatLong = RepeatInterval;
   740	
   741	        DateTimeOffset sTime = fireTimeStartDate.ToUniversalTime();
   742	        IntervalUnit repeatUnit = RepeatIntervalUnit;
   743	        long jumpCount = 0;
   744	        if (repeatUnit == IntervalUnit.Second)
   745	        {
   746	            jumpCount = secondsAfterStart / repeatLong;
   747	            if (secondsAfterStart % repeatLong != 0)
   748	            {
   749	                jumpCount++;
   750	            }
   751	
   752	            sTime = sTime.AddSeconds(RepeatInterval * (int) jumpCount);
   753	            fireTime = TimeZoneUtil.ConvertTime(sTime, TimeZone);
   754	        }
   755	        else if (repeatUnit == IntervalUnit.Minute)
   756	        {
   757	            jumpCount = secondsAfterStart / (repeatLong * 60L);
   758	            if (secondsAfterStart % (repeatLong * 60L) != 0)
   759	            {
   760	                jumpCount++;
   761	            }
   762	            sTime = sTime.AddMinutes(RepeatInterval * (int) jumpCount);
   763	            fireTime = TimeZoneUtil.ConvertTime(sTime, TimeZone);
   764	        }
   765	        else if (repeatUnit == IntervalUnit.Hour)
   766	        {
   767	            jumpCount = secondsAfterStart / (repeatLong * 60L * 60L);
   768	            if (secondsAfterStart % (repeatLong * 60L * 60L) != 0)
   769	            {
   770	                jumpCount++;
   771	            }
   772	            sTime = sTime.AddHours(RepeatInterval * (int) jumpCount);
   773	            fireTime = TimeZoneUtil.ConvertTime(sTime, TimeZone);
   774	        }
   775	
   776	        // g. Check if we've exceeded the per-day repeat count.
   777	        if (repeatCount != RepeatIndefinitely && jumpCount > repeatCount)
   778	        {
   779	            fireTime = AdvanceToNextDayOfWeekIfNecessary(fireTime.Value, true);
   780	            if (fireTime is null)
   781	            {
   782	                return null;
   783	            }
   784	            fireTime = startTimeOfDay.GetTimeOfDayForDate(fireTime);
   785	            return fireTime?.ToUniversalTime();
   786	        }
   787	
   788	        // h. Ensure this new fireTime is within the day, or else we need to advance to next day.
   789	        if (fireTime > fireTimeEndDate)
   790	        {
   791	            fireTime = AdvanceToNextDayOfWeekIfNecessary(fireTime.Value, IsSameDay(fireTime.Value, fireTimeEndDate));
   792	            // make sure we hit the startTimeOfDay on the new day
   793	            fireTime = startTimeOfDay.GetTimeOfDayForDate(fireTime);
   794	        }
   795	
   796	        // i. Return calculated fireTime.
   797	        return fireTime?.ToUniversalTime();
   798	    }
   799	
   800	    private bool IsSameDay(DateTimeOffset d1, DateTimeOffset d2)
   801	    {
   802	        DateTimeOffset c1 = CreateCalendarTime(d1);
   803	        DateTimeOffset c2 = CreateCalendarTime(d2);
   804	
   805	        return c1.Date == c2.Date;
   806	    }
   807	
   808	    /// <summary>
   809	    /// Given fireTime time determine if it is on a valid day of week. If so, simply return it unaltered,
   810	    /// if not, advance to the next valid week day, and set the time of day to the start time of day.
   811	    /// </summary>
   812	    /// <param name="fireTime">given next fireTime.</param>
   813	    /// <param name="forceToAdvanceNextDay">flag to whether to advance day without check existing week day. This scenario
   814	    /// can happen when a caller determine fireTime has passed the endTimeOfDay that fireTime should move to next day anyway.
   815	    /// </param>
   816	    /// <returns>a next day fireTime.</returns>
   817	    private DateTimeOffset? AdvanceToNextDayOfWeekIfNecessary(DateTimeOffset fireTime, bool forceToAdvanceNextDay)
   818	    {
   819	        // a. Advance or adjust to next dayOfWeek if need to first, starting next day with startTimeOfDay.
   820	        TimeOfDay startTimeOfDay = StartTimeOfDay;
   821	        // Get converted start date based on fireTime; fireTime already has the offset applied
   822	        DateTimeOffset fireTimeStartDate = startTimeOfDay.GetTimeOfDayForDate(fireTime);
   823	        DateTimeOffset fireTimeStartDateCal = fireTimeStartDate;
   824	        DayOfWeek dayOfWeekOfFireTime = fireTimeStartDateCal.DayOfWeek;
   825	
   826	        // b2. We need to advance to another day if isAfterTimePassEndTimeOfDay is true, or dayOfWeek is not set.
   827	        var daysOfWeek = new HashSet<DayOfWeek>(DaysOfWeek);
   828	        if (forceToAdvanceNextDay || !daysOfWeek.Contains(dayOfWeekOfFireTime))
   829	        {
   830	            // Advance one day at a time until next available date.
   831	            for (int i = 1; i <= 7; i++)
   832	            {
   833	                fireTimeStartDateCal = fireTimeStartDateCal.AddDays(1);
   834	                dayOfWeekOfFireTime = fireTimeStartDateCal.DayOfWeek;
   835	                if (daysOfWeek.Contains(dayOfWeekOfFireTime))
   836	                {
   837	                    fireTime = fireTimeStartDateCal;
   838	                    // apply timezone for this date & time
   839	                    fireTime = new DateTimeOffset(fireTime.DateTime, TimeZoneUtil.GetUtcOffset(fireTime, TimeZone));
   840	                    break;
   841	                }
   842	            }
   843	        }
   844	
   845	        // Check fireTime not pass the endTime
   846	        DateTimeOffset? endTime = EndTimeUtc;
   847	
   848	        if (endTime is not null && fireTime > endTime.Value)
   849	        {
   850	            return null;
   851	        }
   852	
   853	        return fireTime;
   854	    }
   855	
   856	    /// <summary>
   857	    /// Returns the final time at which the <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger" /> will
   858	    /// fire, if there is no end time set, null will be returned.
   859	    /// </summary>
   860	    /// <remarks>Note that the return time may be in the past.</remarks>
   861	    /// <returns></returns>
   862	    public override DateTimeOffset? FinalFireTimeUtc
   863	    {
   864	        get
   865	        {
   866	            if (complete || EndTimeUtc is null)
   867	            {
   868	                return null;
   869	            }
   870	
   871	            // We have an endTime, we still need to check to see if there is a endTimeOfDay if that's applicable.
   872	            DateTimeOffset? endTime = EndTimeUtc;
   873	            DateTimeOffset? endTimeOfDayDate = endTimeOfDay?.GetTimeOfDayForDate(endTime);
   874	            if (endTime < endTimeOfDayDate)
   875	            {
   876	                endTime = endTimeOfDayDate;
   877	            }
   878	            return endTime;
   879	        }
   880	    }
   881	
   882	    /// <summary>
   883	    /// Determines whether or not the <see cref="IDailyTimeIntervalTrigger" /> will occur
   884	    /// again.
   885	    /// </summary>
   886	    /// <returns></returns>
   887	    public override bool GetMayFireAgain()
   888	    {
   889	        return GetNextFireTimeUtc() is not null;
   890	    }
   891	
   892	    /// <summary>
   893	    /// Validates whether the properties of the <see cref="IJobDetail" /> are
   894	    /// valid for submission into a <see cref="IScheduler" />.
   895	    /// </summary>
   896	    public override void Validate()
   897	    {
   898	        base.Validate();
   899	
   900	        if (repeatIntervalUnit != IntervalUnit.Second && repeatIntervalUnit != IntervalUnit.Minute && repeatIntervalUnit != IntervalUnit.Hour)
   901	        {
   902	            Throw.SchedulerException("Invalid repeat IntervalUnit (must be Second, Minute or Hour).");
   903	        }
   904	        if (repeatInterval < 1)
   905	        {
   906	            Throw.SchedulerException("Repeat Interval cannot be zero.");
   907	        }
   908	
   909	        // Ensure interval does not exceed 24 hours
   910	        const long SecondsInHour = 24 * 60 * 60L;
   911	        if (repeatIntervalUnit == IntervalUnit.Second && repeatInterval > SecondsInHour)
   912	        {
   913	            Throw.SchedulerException("repeatInterval can not exceed 24 hours (" + SecondsInHour + " seconds). Given " + repeatInterval);
   914	        }
   915	        if (repeatIntervalUnit == IntervalUnit.Minute && repeatInterval > SecondsInHour / 60L)
   916	        {
   917	            Throw.SchedulerException("repeatInterval can not exceed 24 hours (" + SecondsInHour / 60L + " minutes). Given " + repeatInterval);
   918	        }
   919	        if (repeatIntervalUnit == IntervalUnit.Hour && repeatInterval > 24)
   920	        {
   921	            Throw.SchedulerException("repeatInterval can not exceed 24 hours. Given " + repeatInterval + " hours.");
   922	        }
   923	
   924	        // Ensure timeOfDay is in order.
   925	        // NOTE: We allow startTimeOfDay to be set equal to endTimeOfDay so the repeatCount can be set to 1.
   926	        if (EndTimeOfDay is not null
   927	            && !StartTimeOfDay.Equals(EndTimeOfDay)
   928	            && !StartTimeOfDay.Before(EndTimeOfDay))
   929	        {
   930	            Throw.SchedulerException($"StartTimeOfDay {startTimeOfDay} should not come after endTimeOfDay {endTimeOfDay}");
   931	        }
   932	    }
   933	
   934	    /// <summary>
   935	    /// The days of the week upon which to fire.
   936	    /// </summary>
   937	    /// <returns>
   938	    /// A Set containing the integers representing the days of the week, per the values 0-6 as defined by
   939	    /// DayOfWees.Sunday - DayOfWeek.Saturday.
   940	    /// </returns>
   941	    public IReadOnlyCollection<DayOfWeek> DaysOfWeek
   942	    {
   943	        get
   944	        {
   945	            if (daysOfWeek is null)
   946	            {
   947	                daysOfWeek = new HashSet<DayOfWeek>(DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder.AllDaysOfTheWeek);
   948	            }
   949	            return daysOfWeek;
   950	        }
   951	
   952	        set
   953	        {
   954	            if (value is null || value.Count == 0)
   955	            {
   956	                Throw.ArgumentException("DaysOfWeek set must be a set that contains at least one day.");
   957	            }
   958	            if (value.Count == 0)
   959	            {
   960	                Throw.ArgumentException("DaysOfWeek set must contain at least one day.");
   961	            }
   962	
   963	            daysOfWeek = new HashSet<DayOfWeek>(value);
   964	        }
   965	    }
   966	
   967	    /// <summary>
   968	    /// The time of day to start firing at the given interval.
   969	    /// </summary>
   970	    public TimeOfDay StartTimeOfDay
   971	    {
   972	        get
   973	        {
   974	            if (startTimeOfDay is null)
   975	            {
   976	                startTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(0, 0, 0);
   977	            }
   978	            return startTimeOfDay;
   979	        }
   980	        set
   981	        {
   982	            if (value is null)
   983	            {
   984	                Throw.ArgumentException("Start time of day cannot be null");
   985	            }
   986	
   987	            TimeOfDay eTime = EndTimeOfDay;
   988	            if (eTime is not null && eTime.Before(value))
   989	            {
   990	                Throw.ArgumentException("End time of day cannot be before start time of day");
   991	            }
   992	
   993	            startTimeOfDay = value;
   994	        }
   995	    }
   996	
   997	    /// <summary>
   998	    /// The time of day to complete firing at the given interval.
   999	    /// </summary>
  1000	    public TimeOfDay EndTimeOfDay
  1001	    {
  1002	        get => endTimeOfDay;
  1003	        set
  1004	        {
  1005	            if (value is null)
  1006	            {
  1007	                Throw.ArgumentException("End time of day cannot be null");
  1008	            }
  1009	
  1010	            TimeOfDay sTime = StartTimeOfDay;
  1011	            if (sTime is not null && value.Before(sTime))
  1012	            {
  1013	                Throw.ArgumentException("End time of day cannot be before start time of day");
  1014	            }
  1015	            endTimeOfDay = value;
  1016	        }
  1017	    }
  1018	
  1019	    /// <summary>
  1020	    /// Get a <see cref="IScheduleBuilder" /> that is configured to produce a
  1021	    /// schedule identical to this trigger's schedule.
  1022	    /// </summary>
  1023	    /// <returns></returns>
  1024	    /// <see cref="TriggerBuilder"/>
  1025	    public override IScheduleBuilder GetScheduleBuilder()
  1026	    {
  1027	        DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder cb = DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder.Create()
  1028	            .WithInterval(RepeatInterval, RepeatIntervalUnit)
  1029	            .OnDaysOfTheWeek(DaysOfWeek)
  1030	            .StartingDailyAt(StartTimeOfDay)
  1031	            .EndingDailyAt(EndTimeOfDay)
  1032	            .WithRepeatCount(RepeatCount)
  1033	            .InTimeZone(TimeZone);
  1034	
  1035	        switch (MisfireInstruction)
  1036	        {
  1037	            case Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.DoNothing:
  1038	                cb.WithMisfireHandlingInstructionDoNothing();
  1039	                break;
  1040	            case Quartz.MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.FireOnceNow:
  1041	                cb.WithMisfireHandlingInstructionFireAndProceed();
  1042	                break;
  1043	            case Quartz.MisfireInstruction.IgnoreMisfirePolicy:
  1044	                cb.WithMisfireHandlingInstructionIgnoreMisfires();
  1045	                break;
  1046	        }
  1047	
  1048	        return cb;
  1049	    }
  1050	
  1051	    /// <summary>
  1052	    /// Tells whether this Trigger instance can handle events
  1053	    /// in millisecond precision.
  1054	    /// </summary>
  1055	    public override bool HasMillisecondPrecision => true;
  1056	}

    32	/// <summary>
    33	/// Unit test for <see cref="DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl"/>.
    34	/// </summary>
    35	/// <author>Zemian Deng saltnlight5@gmail.com</author>
    36	/// <author>Nuno Maia (.NET)</author>
    37	[TestFixture]
    38	public class DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImplTest
    39	{
    40	    [Test]
    41	    public void TestNormalExample()
    42	    {
    43	        DateTimeOffset startTime = DateBuilder.DateOf(0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011);
    44	        TimeOfDay startTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(8, 0, 0);
    45	        TimeOfDay endTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(11, 0, 0);
    46	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
    47	        {
    48	            StartTimeUtc = startTime.ToUniversalTime(),
    49	            StartTimeOfDay = startTimeOfDay,
    50	            EndTimeOfDay = endTimeOfDay,
    51	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Minute,
    52	            RepeatInterval = 72 // this interval will give three firings per day (8:00, 9:12, and 10:24)
    53	        };
    54	
    55	        var fireTimes = TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimes(trigger, null, 48);
    56	        Assert.Multiple(() =>
    57	        {
    58	            Assert.That(fireTimes, Has.Count.EqualTo(48));
    59	            Assert.That(fireTimes[0], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)));
    60	            Assert.That(fireTimes[47], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(10, 24, 0, 16, 1, 2011)));
    61	        });
    62	    }
    63	
    64	    [Test]
    65	    public void TestQuartzCalendarExclusion()
    66	    {
    67	        DateTimeOffset startTime = DateBuilder.DateOf(0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011);
    68	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
    69	        {
    70	            StartTimeUtc = startTime.ToUniversalTime(),
    71	            StartTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(8, 0),
    72	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Minute,
    73	            RepeatInterval = 60
    74	        };
    75	
    76	        CronCalendar cronCal = new CronCalendar("* * 9-12 * * ?"); // exclude 9-12
    77	        var fireTimes = TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimes(trigger, cronCal, 48);
    78	        Assert.Multiple(() =>
    79	        {
    80	            Assert.That(fireTimes.Count, Is.EqualTo(48));
    81	            Assert.That(fireTimes[0], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)));
    82	            Assert.That(fireTimes[1], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(13, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)));
    83	            Assert.That(fireTimes[47], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(23, 0, 0, 4, 1, 2011)));
    84	        });
    85	    }

    87	    [Test]
    88	    public void TestValidateTimeOfDayOrder()
    89	    {
    90	        Assert.Throws<ArgumentException>(() =>
    91	            new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
    92	            {
    93	                StartTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(12, 0, 0),
    94	                EndTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(8, 0, 0)
    95	            }, "End time of day cannot be before start time of day");
    96	    }
    97	
    98	    [Test]
    99	    public void TestValidateInterval()
   100	    {
   101	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
   102	        {
   103	            Key = new TriggerKey("test", "test"),
   104	            JobKey = JobKey.Create("test"),
   105	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Hour,
   106	            RepeatInterval = 25
   107	        };
   108	
   109	        Assert.Throws<SchedulerException>(trigger.Validate, "repeatInterval can not exceed 24 hours. Given 25 hours.");
   110	
   111	        trigger.RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Minute;
   112	        trigger.RepeatInterval = 60 * 25;
   113	        Assert.Throws<SchedulerException>(trigger.Validate, "repeatInterval can not exceed 24 hours (86400 seconds). Given 90000");
   114	
   115	        trigger.RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Second;
   116	        trigger.RepeatInterval = 60 * 60 * 25;
   117	
   118	        Assert.Throws<SchedulerException>(trigger.Validate, "repeatInterval can not exceed 24 hours (86400 seconds). Given 90000");
   119	
   120	        Assert.Throws<ArgumentException>(delegate { trigger.RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Day; }, "Invalid repeat IntervalUnit (must be Second, Minute or Hour)");
   121	
   122	        trigger.RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Second;
   123	        Assert.Throws<ArgumentException>(() => trigger.RepeatInterval = 0, "Repeat Interval cannot be zero.");
   124	    }

   190	    [Test]
   191	    public void TestStartTimeBeforeStartTimeOfDayOnInvalidDay()
   192	    {
   193	        DateTimeOffset startTime = dateOf(0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011); // Jan 1, 2011 was a saturday...
   194	        TimeOfDay startTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(8, 0, 0);
   195	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl();
   196	        var daysOfWeek = new List<DayOfWeek>
   197	        {
   198	            DayOfWeek.Monday,
   199	            DayOfWeek.Tuesday,
   200	            DayOfWeek.Wednesday,
   201	            DayOfWeek.Thursday,
   202	            DayOfWeek.Friday
   203	        };
   204	        trigger.DaysOfWeek = daysOfWeek;
   205	        trigger.StartTimeUtc = startTime.ToUniversalTime();
   206	        trigger.StartTimeOfDay = startTimeOfDay;
   207	        trigger.RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Minute;
   208	        trigger.RepeatInterval = 60;
   209	
   210	        Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(6, 0, 0, 22, 5, 2010)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 3, 1, 2011)));
   211	
   212	        var fireTimes = TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimes(trigger, null, 48);
   213	        Assert.Multiple(() =>
   214	        {
   215	            Assert.That(fireTimes, Has.Count.EqualTo(48));
   216	            Assert.That(fireTimes[0], Is.EqualTo(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 3, 1, 2011)));
   217	            Assert.That(fireTimes[47], Is.EqualTo(dateOf(23, 0, 0, 5, 1, 2011)));
   218	        });
   219	    }

   245	    {

   247	        DateTimeOffset endTime = DateBuilder.DateOf(16, 0, 0, 2, 1, 2011);
   248	        TimeOfDay endTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(17, 0, 0);
   249	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
   250	        {
   251	            StartTimeUtc = startTime.ToUniversalTime(),
   252	            EndTimeUtc = endTime.ToUniversalTime(),
   253	            EndTimeOfDay = endTimeOfDay,
   254	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Minute,
   255	            RepeatInterval = 60
   256	        };

   258	        var fireTimes = TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimes(trigger, null, 48);
   259	        Assert.Multiple(() =>
   260	        {

   264	            Assert.That(fireTimes[34], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(16, 0, 0, 2, 1, 2011)));
   265	        });

   294	    public void TestTimeOfDayWithStartTime()
   295	    {
   296	        DateTimeOffset startTime = DateBuilder.DateOf(0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011);
   297	        TimeOfDay startTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(8, 0, 0);
   298	        TimeOfDay endTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(17, 0, 0);
   299	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
   300	        {
   301	            StartTimeUtc = startTime.ToUniversalTime(),
   302	            StartTimeOfDay = startTimeOfDay,
   303	            EndTimeOfDay = endTimeOfDay,
   304	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Minute,
   305	            RepeatInterval = 60
   306	        };
   307	
   308	        var fireTimes = TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimes(trigger, null, 48);
   309	        Assert.Multiple(() =>
   310	        {
   311	            Assert.That(fireTimes, Has.Count.EqualTo(48));
   312	            Assert.That(fireTimes[0], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)));
   313	            Assert.That(fireTimes[9], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(17, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011))); // The 10th hours is the end of day.
   314	            Assert.That(fireTimes[47], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(15, 0, 0, 5, 1, 2011)));
   315	        });

   396	    [Test]
   397	    public void TestMonThroughFri()
   398	    {
   399	        IReadOnlyCollection<DayOfWeek> daysOfWeek = DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder.MondayThroughFriday;
   400	        DateTimeOffset startTime = DateBuilder.DateOf(0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011); // SAT(7)
   401	        TimeOfDay startTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(8, 0, 0);
   402	        TimeOfDay endTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(17, 0, 0);
   403	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
   404	        {
   405	            StartTimeUtc = startTime.ToUniversalTime(),
   406	            StartTimeOfDay = startTimeOfDay,
   407	            EndTimeOfDay = endTimeOfDay,
   408	            DaysOfWeek = daysOfWeek,
   409	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Minute,
   410	            RepeatInterval = 60
   411	        };
   412	
   413	        var fireTimes = TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimes(trigger, null, 48);
   414	        
   415	        Assert.Multiple(() =>
   416	        {
   417	            Assert.That(fireTimes, Has.Count.EqualTo(48));
   418	            Assert.That(fireTimes[0], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 3, 1, 2011)));
   419	            Assert.That(fireTimes[0].LocalDateTime.DayOfWeek, Is.EqualTo(DayOfWeek.Monday));
   420	            Assert.That(fireTimes[10], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 4, 1, 2011)));
   421	            Assert.That(fireTimes[10].LocalDateTime.DayOfWeek, Is.EqualTo(DayOfWeek.Tuesday));
   422	            Assert.That(fireTimes[47], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(15, 0, 0, 7, 1, 2011)));
   423	            Assert.That(fireTimes[47].LocalDateTime.DayOfWeek, Is.EqualTo(DayOfWeek.Friday));
   424	        });
   425	    }

   457	    [TestCase(-14)]
   458	    [TestCase(0)]
   459	    [TestCase(10)]
   460	    public void TestMonOnly(int tzOffsetHours)
   461	    {
   462	        var daysOfWeek = new HashSet<DayOfWeek>
   463	        {
   464	            DayOfWeek.Monday
   465	        };
   466	        DateTimeOffset startTime = new DateTimeOffset(2011, 1, 1, 0, 0, 0, TimeSpan.FromHours(tzOffsetHours)); // SAT(7)
   467	        TimeOfDay startTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(8, 0, 0);
   468	        TimeOfDay endTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(17, 0, 0);
   469	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
   470	        {
   471	            StartTimeUtc = startTime.ToUniversalTime(),
   472	            StartTimeOfDay = startTimeOfDay,
   473	            EndTimeOfDay = endTimeOfDay,
   474	            DaysOfWeek = daysOfWeek,
   475	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Minute,
   476	            RepeatInterval = 60
   477	        };
   478	
   479	        var fireTimes = TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimes(trigger, null, 48);
   480	        Assert.Multiple(() =>{
   481	            Assert.That(fireTimes, Has.Count.EqualTo(48));
   482	            Assert.That(fireTimes[0], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 3, 1, 2011)));
   483	            Assert.That(fireTimes[0].LocalDateTime.DayOfWeek, Is.EqualTo(DayOfWeek.Monday));
   484	            Assert.That(fireTimes[10], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 10, 1, 2011)));
   485	            Assert.That(fireTimes[10].LocalDateTime.DayOfWeek, Is.EqualTo(DayOfWeek.Monday));
   486	            Assert.That(fireTimes[47], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(15, 0, 0, 31, 1, 2011)));
   487	            Assert.That(fireTimes[47].LocalDateTime.DayOfWeek, Is.EqualTo(DayOfWeek.Monday));
   488	        });
   489	    }

   595	    [Test]
   596	    public void TestRepeatCount()
   597	    {
   598	        DateTimeOffset startTime = DateBuilder.DateOf(0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011);
   599	        TimeOfDay startTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(8, 0, 0);
   600	        TimeOfDay endTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(11, 0, 0);
   601	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
   602	        {
   603	            StartTimeUtc = startTime.ToUniversalTime(),
   604	            StartTimeOfDay = startTimeOfDay,
   605	            EndTimeOfDay = endTimeOfDay,
   606	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Minute,
   607	            RepeatInterval = 72,
   608	            RepeatCount = 7
   609	        };
   610	
   611	        // repeatCount=7 allows 8 fires/day, but 8:00-11:00 with 72min interval only allows 3/day
   612	        // so endTimeOfDay is the effective limiter; trigger continues across days
   613	        var fireTimes = TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimes(trigger, null, 48);
   614	        Assert.Multiple(() =>
   615	        {
   616	            Assert.That(fireTimes, Has.Count.EqualTo(48));
   617	            Assert.That(fireTimes[0], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)));
   618	            Assert.That(fireTimes[47], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(10, 24, 0, 16, 1, 2011)));
   619	        });
   620	    }

   622	    [Test]
   623	    public void TestRepeatCount0()
   624	    {
   625	        DateTimeOffset startTime = DateBuilder.DateOf(0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011);
   626	        TimeOfDay startTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(8, 0, 0);
   627	        TimeOfDay endTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(11, 0, 0);
   628	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
   629	        {
   630	            StartTimeUtc = startTime.ToUniversalTime(),
   631	            StartTimeOfDay = startTimeOfDay,
   632	            EndTimeOfDay = endTimeOfDay,
   633	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Minute,
   634	            RepeatInterval = 72,
   635	            RepeatCount = 0
   636	        };
   637	
   638	        // repeatCount=0 means 1 fire per day (at startTimeOfDay), continuing daily
   639	        var fireTimes = TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimes(trigger, null, 5);
   640	        Assert.Multiple(() =>
   641	        {
   642	            Assert.That(fireTimes, Has.Count.EqualTo(5));
   643	            Assert.That(fireTimes[0], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)));
   644	            Assert.That(fireTimes[1], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 2, 1, 2011)));
   645	            Assert.That(fireTimes[2], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 3, 1, 2011)));
   646	            Assert.That(fireTimes[3], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 4, 1, 2011)));
   647	            Assert.That(fireTimes[4], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 5, 1, 2011)));
   648	        });
   649	    }

   651	    [Test]
   652	    public void TestRepeatCountLimitsPerDay()
   653	    {
   654	        DateTimeOffset startTime = DateBuilder.DateOf(0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011);
   655	        TimeOfDay startTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(8, 0, 0);
   656	        TimeOfDay endTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(17, 0, 0);
   657	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
   658	        {
   659	            StartTimeUtc = startTime.ToUniversalTime(),
   660	            StartTimeOfDay = startTimeOfDay,
   661	            EndTimeOfDay = endTimeOfDay,
   662	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Hour,
   663	            RepeatInterval = 1,
   664	            RepeatCount = 2 // 3 fires per day: 8:00, 9:00, 10:00
   665	        };
   666	
   667	        var fireTimes = TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimes(trigger, null, 9);
   668	        Assert.Multiple(() =>
   669	        {
   670	            Assert.That(fireTimes, Has.Count.EqualTo(9));
   671	            // Day 1
   672	            Assert.That(fireTimes[0], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)));
   673	            Assert.That(fireTimes[1], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(9, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)));
   674	            Assert.That(fireTimes[2], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(10, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)));
   675	            // Day 2
   676	            Assert.That(fireTimes[3], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 2, 1, 2011)));
   677	            Assert.That(fireTimes[4], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(9, 0, 0, 2, 1, 2011)));
   678	            Assert.That(fireTimes[5], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(10, 0, 0, 2, 1, 2011)));
   679	            // Day 3
   680	            Assert.That(fireTimes[6], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 3, 1, 2011)));
   681	            Assert.That(fireTimes[7], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(9, 0, 0, 3, 1, 2011)));
   682	            Assert.That(fireTimes[8], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(10, 0, 0, 3, 1, 2011)));
   683	        });
   684	    }

   698	            EndTimeOfDay = endTimeOfDay,
   699	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Hour,

   717	    [Test]
   718	    public void TestRepeatCountWithDaysOfWeek()
   719	    {
   720	        // Jan 1 2011 is Saturday
   721	        DateTimeOffset startTime = DateBuilder.DateOf(0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011);
   722	        TimeOfDay startTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(8, 0, 0);
   723	        TimeOfDay endTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(17, 0, 0);
   724	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
   725	        {
   726	            StartTimeUtc = startTime.ToUniversalTime(),
   727	            StartTimeOfDay = startTimeOfDay,
   728	            EndTimeOfDay = endTimeOfDay,
   729	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Hour,
   730	            RepeatInterval = 1,
   731	            RepeatCount = 1, // 2 fires per day
   732	            DaysOfWeek = new HashSet<DayOfWeek> { DayOfWeek.Monday, DayOfWeek.Wednesday, DayOfWeek.Friday }
   733	        };
   734	
   735	        var fireTimes = TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimes(trigger, null, 6);
   736	        Assert.Multiple(() =>
   737	        {
   738	            Assert.That(fireTimes, Has.Count.EqualTo(6));
   739	            // Mon Jan 3
   740	            Assert.That(fireTimes[0], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 3, 1, 2011)));
   741	            Assert.That(fireTimes[1], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(9, 0, 0, 3, 1, 2011)));
   742	            // Wed Jan 5
   743	            Assert.That(fireTimes[2], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 5, 1, 2011)));
   744	            Assert.That(fireTimes[3], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(9, 0, 0, 5, 1, 2011)));
   745	            // Fri Jan 7
   746	            Assert.That(fireTimes[4], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(8, 0, 0, 7, 1, 2011)));
   747	            Assert.That(fireTimes[5], Is.EqualTo(DateBuilder.DateOf(9, 0, 0, 7, 1, 2011)));
   748	        });
   749	    }

   751	    [Test]
   752	    public void TestFollowsTimeZone1()
   753	    {
   754	        TimeZoneInfo est = TimeZoneUtil.FindTimeZoneById("Eastern Standard Time");
   755	
   756	        DateTimeOffset startTime = new DateTimeOffset(2012, 3, 9, 23, 0, 0, TimeSpan.FromHours(-5));
   757	
   758	        TimeOfDay startTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(8, 0, 0);
   759	        TimeOfDay endTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(11, 0, 0);
   760	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
   761	        {
   762	            StartTimeUtc = startTime.ToUniversalTime(),
   763	            StartTimeOfDay = startTimeOfDay,
   764	            EndTimeOfDay = endTimeOfDay,
   765	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Hour,
   766	            RepeatInterval = 1,
   767	            TimeZone = est
   768	        };
   769	
   770	        var fireTimes = TriggerUtils.ComputeFireTimes(trigger, null, 8);
   771	
   772	        DateTimeOffset expected0 = new DateTimeOffset(2012, 3, 10, 8, 0, 0, 0, TimeSpan.FromHours(-5));
   773	        DateTimeOffset expected1 = new DateTimeOffset(2012, 3, 10, 9, 0, 0, 0, TimeSpan.FromHours(-5));
   774	        DateTimeOffset expected2 = new DateTimeOffset(2012, 3, 10, 10, 0, 0, 0, TimeSpan.FromHours(-5));
   775	        DateTimeOffset expected3 = new DateTimeOffset(2012, 3, 10, 11, 0, 0, 0, TimeSpan.FromHours(-5));
   776	
   777	        DateTimeOffset expected4 = new DateTimeOffset(2012, 3, 11, 8, 0, 0, 0, TimeSpan.FromHours(-4));
   778	        DateTimeOffset expected5 = new DateTimeOffset(2012, 3, 11, 9, 0, 0, 0, TimeSpan.FromHours(-4));
   779	        DateTimeOffset expected6 = new DateTimeOffset(2012, 3, 11, 10, 0, 0, 0, TimeSpan.FromHours(-4));
   780	        DateTimeOffset expected7 = new DateTimeOffset(2012, 3, 11, 11, 0, 0, 0, TimeSpan.FromHours(-4));
   781	
   782	        Assert.Multiple(() =>
   783	        {
   784	            Assert.That(fireTimes[0], Is.EqualTo(expected0));
   785	            Assert.That(fireTimes[1], Is.EqualTo(expected1));
   786	            Assert.That(fireTimes[2], Is.EqualTo(expected2));
   787	            Assert.That(fireTimes[3], Is.EqualTo(expected3));
   788	            Assert.That(fireTimes[4], Is.EqualTo(expected4));
   789	            Assert.That(fireTimes[5], Is.EqualTo(expected5));
   790	            Assert.That(fireTimes[6], Is.EqualTo(expected6));
   791	            Assert.That(fireTimes[7], Is.EqualTo(expected7));
   792	        });
   793	    }

   839	    [Test]
   840	    public void DayOfWeekPropertyShouldNotAffectOtherTriggers()
   841	    {
   842	        //make 2 trigger exactly the same
   843	        DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl trigger1 = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
   844	        {
   845	            RepeatInterval = 1,
   846	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Hour
   847	        };
   848	
   849	        DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl trigger2 = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl
   850	        {
   851	            RepeatInterval = 1,
   852	            RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Hour
   853	        };
   854	
   855	        //make an adjustment to only one trigger.
   856	        //I only want mondays now
   857	        trigger1.DaysOfWeek = new List<DayOfWeek>
   858	        {
   859	            DayOfWeek.Monday
   860	        };
   861	
   862	        //check trigger 2 DOW
   863	        //this fails because the reference collection only contains MONDAY b/c it was cleared.
   864	        Assert.Multiple(() =>
   865	        {
   866	            Assert.That(trigger2.DaysOfWeek, Does.Contain(DayOfWeek.Monday));
   867	            Assert.That(trigger2.DaysOfWeek, Does.Contain(DayOfWeek.Tuesday));
   868	            Assert.That(trigger2.DaysOfWeek, Does.Contain(DayOfWeek.Wednesday));
   869	            Assert.That(trigger2.DaysOfWeek, Does.Contain(DayOfWeek.Thursday));
   870	            Assert.That(trigger2.DaysOfWeek, Does.Contain(DayOfWeek.Friday));
   871	            Assert.That(trigger2.DaysOfWeek, Does.Contain(DayOfWeek.Saturday));
   872	            Assert.That(trigger2.DaysOfWeek, Does.Contain(DayOfWeek.Sunday));
   873	        });
   874	    }

   887	
   888	    [Test]
   889	    public void TestGetFireTime()
   890	    {
   891	        DateTime startTime = new DateTime(2011, 1, 1);
   892	        TimeOfDay startTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(8, 0, 0);
   893	        TimeOfDay endTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(13, 0, 0);
   894	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl();
   895	        trigger.StartTimeUtc = startTime;
   896	        trigger.StartTimeOfDay = startTimeOfDay;
   897	        trigger.EndTimeOfDay = endTimeOfDay;
   898	        trigger.RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Hour;
   899	        trigger.RepeatInterval = 1;
   900	
   901	        Assert.Multiple(() =>
   902	        {
   903	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)));
   904	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(7, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)));
   905	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(7, 59, 59, 1, 1, 2011)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)));
   906	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(9, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)));
   907	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(9, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(10, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)));
   908	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(12, 59, 59, 1, 1, 2011)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(13, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)));
   909	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(13, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 2, 1, 2011)));
   910	        });
   911	    }
   912	
   913	    private DateTimeOffset dateOf(int hour, int minute, int second, int dayOfMonth, int month, int year)
   914	    {
   915	        return new DateTime(year, month, dayOfMonth, hour, minute, second);
   916	    }
   917	
   918	    [Test]
   919	    public void TestGetFireTimeWithDateBeforeStartTime()
   920	    {
   921	        DateTime startTime = new DateTime(2012, 1, 1);
   922	        TimeOfDay startTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(8, 0, 0);
   923	        TimeOfDay endTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(13, 0, 0);
   924	        DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl();
   925	        trigger.StartTimeUtc = startTime;
   926	        trigger.StartTimeOfDay = startTimeOfDay;
   927	        trigger.EndTimeOfDay = endTimeOfDay;
   928	        trigger.RepeatIntervalUnit = IntervalUnit.Hour;
   929	        trigger.RepeatInterval = 1;
   930	
   931	        // NOTE that if you pass a date past the startTime, you will get the startTime back!
   932	        Assert.Multiple(() =>
   933	        {
   934	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2012)));
   935	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(7, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2012)));
   936	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(7, 59, 59, 1, 1, 2011)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2012)));
   937	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2012)));
   938	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(9, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2012)));
   939	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(12, 59, 59, 1, 1, 2011)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2012)));
   940	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(13, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2011)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2012)));
   941	
   942	            // Now try some test times at or after startTime
   943	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(0, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2012)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2012)));
   944	            Assert.That(trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(dateOf(13, 0, 0, 1, 1, 2012)), Is.EqualTo(dateOf(8, 0, 0, 2, 1, 2012)));
   945	        });
   946	    }

  1013	    [Category("windowstimezoneid")]
  1014	    public void TestDayLightSaving()
  1015	    {
  1016	        var timeZoneInfo = TZConvert.GetTimeZoneInfo("GMT Standard Time");
  1017	
  1018	        var trigger = DailyTimeIntervalScheduleBuilder.Create()
  1019	            .StartingDailyAt(TimeOfDay.HourAndMinuteOfDay(22, 15))
  1020	            .OnEveryDay()
  1021	            .WithIntervalInHours(24)
  1022	            .WithRepeatCount(9999)
  1023	            .InTimeZone(timeZoneInfo)
  1024	            .Build();
  1025	
  1026	        var first = trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(new DateTimeOffset(2014, 10, 25, 0, 0, 0, TimeSpan.Zero));
  1027	        Assert.That(first, Is.EqualTo(new DateTimeOffset(2014, 10, 25, 22, 15, 0, TimeSpan.FromHours(1))));
  1028	
  1029	        var second = trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(first);
  1030	        Assert.That(second, Is.EqualTo(new DateTimeOffset(2014, 10, 26, 22, 15, 0, TimeSpan.FromHours(0))));
  1031	
  1032	        var third = trigger.GetFireTimeAfter(second);
  1033	        Assert.That(third, Is.EqualTo(new DateTimeOffset(2014, 10, 27, 22, 15, 0, TimeSpan.FromHours(0))));
  1034	    }

  1111	    public void ShouldGetScheduleBuilderWithSameSettingsAsTrigger()
  1112	    {
  1113	        var startTime = DateTimeOffset.UtcNow;
  1114	        var endTime = DateTimeOffset.UtcNow.AddDays(1);
  1115	        var startTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(1, 2, 3);
  1116	        var endTimeOfDay = new TimeOfDay(3, 2, 1);
  1117	        var trigger = new DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl("name", "group", startTime, endTime, startTimeOfDay, endTimeOfDay, IntervalUnit.Hour, 10);
  1118	        trigger.RepeatCount = 12;
  1119	        trigger.DaysOfWeek = new List<DayOfWeek>
  1120	        {
  1121	            DayOfWeek.Thursday
  1122	        };
  1123	        trigger.MisfireInstruction = MisfireInstruction.DailyTimeIntervalTrigger.FireOnceNow;
  1124	        trigger.TimeZone = TimeZoneInfo.Utc;
  1125	
  1126	        var scheduleBuilder = trigger.GetScheduleBuilder();
  1127	
  1128	        var cloned = (DailyTimeIntervalTriggerImpl) scheduleBuilder.Build();
  1129	        Assert.Multiple(() =>
  1130	        {
  1131	            Assert.That(trigger.DaysOfWeek, Is.EqualTo(cloned.DaysOfWeek).AsCollection);
  1132	            Assert.That(cloned.RepeatCount, Is.EqualTo(trigger.RepeatCount));
  1133	            Assert.That(cloned.RepeatInterval, Is.EqualTo(trigger.RepeatInterval));
  1134	            Assert.That(cloned.RepeatIntervalUnit, Is.EqualTo(trigger.RepeatIntervalUnit));
  1135	            Assert.That(cloned.StartTimeOfDay, Is.EqualTo(trigger.StartTimeOfDay));
  1136	            Assert.That(cloned.EndTimeOfDay, Is.EqualTo(trigger.EndTimeOfDay));
  1137	            Assert.That(cloned.TimeZone, Is.EqualTo(trigger.TimeZone));
  1138	        });
  1139	    }
